import requests

header_data= {
    'accept': 'application/json',
    'Authorization': 'VXgWV/f5wELzapZjJF7FEqqtFhPbNA8KBIWia3SXOCvY+CXEUok1DhybfbP4USE/g2b/QYT62C2mw3zcSWj2pg==',
}

param_data = (
    ('page', '1'),
    ('perPage', '1000'),
    ('serviceKey', 'VXgWV/f5wELzapZjJF7FEqqtFhPbNA8KBIWia3SXOCvY+CXEUok1DhybfbP4USE/g2b/QYT62C2mw3zcSWj2pg=='),
)

url = 'https://api.odcloud.kr/api/15069309/v1/uddi:973ad0df-617a-4565-8e82-8ea7869e75d4'
## decode key가 적용되었음.
## api마다 연결이 되지 않는다고 한다면, encode, decode를 바꾸어 테스트해볼 것.
response = requests.get(url, headers=header_data, params=param_data)

In [58]:
total_row = []
for no in range(1000):
    com = data_values[no]['언론사']
    content = data_values[no]['본문']
    addr = data_values[no]['원본주소']
    date = data_values[no]['일자']
    field = data_values[no]['통합 분류1']
    title = data_values[no]['제목']
    one_row = []
    one_row.append(title)
    one_row.append(content)
    one_row.append(field)
    one_row.append(date)
    one_row.append(addr)
    one_row.append(com)
    #print(one_row)
    total_row.append(one_row)
    print('전체기사수 >> ', len(total_row))
